                        "# survey_app.py\n\"\"\"\nA minimal Python web application using FastAPI (backend) and React (frontend) for:\n- Survey creation and response capture\n- Data analysis via radar charts and heatmaps (API endpoints)\n- PDF/CSV report generation\n- RESTful APIs for survey management\n\nFrontend code (React) is provided as a separate folder structure below.\n\nRequirements:\n- fastapi\n- uvicorn\n- sqlalchemy\n- pydantic\n- pandas\n- matplotlib\n- reportlab\n- python-multipart\n\nInstall dependencies:\npip install fastapi uvicorn sqlalchemy pydantic pandas matplotlib reportlab python-multipart\n\nRun the backend:\nuvicorn survey_app:app --reload\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException, UploadFile, File, Form\nfrom fastapi.responses import FileResponse\nfrom fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware\nfrom pydantic import BaseModel\nfrom sqlalchemy import create_engine, Column, Integer, String, Text, ForeignKey, JSON\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker, declarative_base, relationship\nimport pandas as pd\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\nfrom reportlab.platypus import SimpleDocTemplate, Paragraph, Spacer, Table\nfrom reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter\nfrom reportlab.lib.styles import getSampleStyleSheet\nimport io\nimport json\nimport os\n\n# Database setup\nDATABASE_URL = \"sqlite:///./survey.db\"\nengine = create_engine(DATABASE_URL, connect_args={\"check_same_thread\": False})\nSessionLocal = sessionmaker(bind=engine)\nBase = declarative_base()\n\n# Models\nclass Survey(Base):\n    __tablename__ = \"surveys\"\n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    title = Column(String, index=True)\n    description = Column(Text)\n    questions = Column(JSON)  # List of questions\n\nclass Response(Base):\n    __tablename__ = \"responses\"\n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    survey_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey(\"surveys.id\"))\n    answers = Column(JSON)  # Dict: {question_id: answer}\n    survey = relationship(\"Survey\")\n\nBase.metadata.create_all(bind=engine)\n\n# Pydantic schemas\nclass SurveyCreate(BaseModel):\n    title: str\n    description: str\n    questions: list  # List of dicts: [{\"id\": 1, \"text\": \"...\", \"type\": \"scale|text|choice\", \"options\": [...]}, ...]\n\nclass SurveyOut(BaseModel):\n    id: int\n    title: str\n    description: str\n    questions: list\n\nclass ResponseCreate(BaseModel):\n    survey_id: int\n    answers: dict  # {question_id: answer}\n\nclass ResponseOut(BaseModel):\n    id: int\n    survey_id: int\n    answers: dict\n\n# FastAPI app\napp = FastAPI(title=\"Survey MVP API\")\n\n# CORS for frontend\napp.add_middleware(\n    CORSMiddleware,\n    allow_origins=[\"*\"],  # Set to your frontend origin in production\n    allow_credentials=True,\n    allow_methods=[\"*\"],\n    allow_headers=[\"*\"],\n)\n\n# API Endpoints\n\n@app.post(\"/surveys/\", response_model=SurveyOut)\ndef create_survey(survey: SurveyCreate):\n    db = SessionLocal()\n    db_survey = Survey(\n        title=survey.title,\n        description=survey.description,\n        questions=survey.questions\n    )\n    db.add(db_survey)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(db_survey)\n    db.close()\n    return SurveyOut(\n        id=db_survey.id,\n        title=db_survey.title,\n        description=db_survey.description,\n        questions=db_survey.questions\n    )\n\n@app.get(\"/surveys/\", response_model=list[SurveyOut])\ndef list_surveys():\n    db = SessionLocal()\n    surveys = db.query(Survey).all()\n    db.close()\n    return [\n        SurveyOut(\n            id=s.id,\n            title=s.title,\n            description=s.description,\n            questions=s.questions\n        ) for s in surveys\n    ]\n\n@app.get(\"/surveys/{survey_id}\", response_model=SurveyOut)\ndef get_survey(survey_id: int):\n    db = SessionLocal()\n    survey = db.query(Survey).filter(Survey.id == survey_id).first()\n    db.close()\n    if not survey:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=\"Survey not found\")\n    return SurveyOut(\n        id=survey.id,\n        title=survey.title,\n        description=survey.description,\n        questions=survey.questions\n    )\n\n@app.post(\"/responses/\", response_model=ResponseOut)\ndef submit_response(response: ResponseCreate):\n    db = SessionLocal()\n    db_response = Response(\n        survey_id=response.survey_id,\n        answers=response.answers\n    )\n    db.add(db_response)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(db_response)\n    db.close()\n    return ResponseOut(\n        id=db_response.id,\n        survey_id=db_response.survey_id,\n        answers=db_response.answers\n    )\n\n@app.get(\"/responses/{survey_id}\", response_model=list[ResponseOut])\ndef list_responses(survey_id: int):\n    db = SessionLocal()\n    responses = db.query(Response).filter(Response.survey_id == survey_id).all()\n    db.close()\n    return [\n        ResponseOut(\n            id=r.id,\n            survey_id=r.survey_id,\n            answers=r.answers\n        ) for r in responses\n    ]\n\n# Data Analysis Endpoints\n\n@app.get(\"/analysis/radar/{survey_id}\")\ndef radar_chart(survey_id: int):\n    \"\"\"\n    Returns a radar chart PNG for scale-type questions.\n    \"\"\"\n    db = SessionLocal()\n    survey = db.query(Survey).filter(Survey.id == survey_id).first()\n    responses = db.query(Response).filter(Response.survey_id == survey_id).all()\n    db.close()\n    if not survey or not responses:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=\"Survey or responses not found\")\n\n    # Only scale-type questions\n    scale_questions = [q for q in survey.questions if q.get(\"type\") == \"scale\"]\n    labels = [q[\"text\"] for q in scale_questions]\n    q_ids = [str(q[\"id\"]) for q in scale_questions]\n\n    # Aggregate mean per question\n    data = []\n    for qid in q_ids:\n        vals = []\n        for r in responses:\n            ans = r.answers.get(qid)\n            if isinstance(ans, (int, float)):\n                vals.append(ans)\n        data.append(sum(vals)/len(vals) if vals else 0)\n\n    # Radar plot\n    angles = [n / float(len(labels)) * 2 * 3.14159 for n in range(len(labels))]\n    data += data[:1]\n    angles += angles[:1]\n\n    fig, ax = plt.subplots(subplot_kw=dict(polar=True))\n    ax.plot(angles, data, linewidth=2, linestyle='solid')\n    ax.fill(angles, data, alpha=0.25)\n    ax.set_xticks(angles[:-1])\n    ax.set_xticklabels(labels)\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    buf = io.BytesIO()\n    plt.savefig(buf, format=\"png\")\n    plt.close(fig)\n    buf.seek(0)\n    return FileResponse(buf, media_type=\"image/png\")\n\n@app.get(\"/analysis/heatmap/{survey_id}\")\ndef heatmap(survey_id: int):\n    \"\"\"\n    Returns a heatmap PNG for choice-type questions.\n    \"\"\"\n    db = SessionLocal()\n    survey = db.query(Survey).filter(Survey.id == survey_id).first()\n    responses = db.query(Response).filter(Response.survey_id == survey_id).all()\n    db.close()\n    if not survey or not responses:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=\"Survey or responses not found\")\n\n    choice_questions = [q for q in survey.questions if q.get(\"type\") == \"choice\"]\n    q_ids = [str(q[\"id\"]) for q in choice_questions]\n    options = [q.get(\"options\", []) for q in choice_questions]\n\n    # Build frequency matrix\n    freq = []\n    for idx, qid in enumerate(q_ids):\n        opts = options[idx]\n        counts = [0]*len(opts)\n        for r in responses:\n            ans = r.answers.get(qid)\n            if ans in opts:\n                counts[opts.index(ans)] += 1\n        freq.append(counts)\n    df = pd.DataFrame(freq, index=[q[\"text\"] for q in choice_questions], columns=[opt for opts in options for opt in opts])\n\n    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(8, 4))\n    cax = ax.matshow(df.values, cmap='YlOrRd')\n    plt.xticks(range(df.shape[1]), df.columns, rotation=90)\n    plt.yticks(range(df.shape[0]), df.index)\n    plt.colorbar(cax)\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    buf = io.BytesIO()\n    plt.savefig(buf, format=\"png\")\n    plt.close(fig)\n    buf.seek(0)\n    return FileResponse(buf, media_type=\"image/png\")\n\n# Report Generation Endpoints\n\n@app.get(\"/report/csv/{survey_id}\")\ndef survey_csv(survey_id: int):\n    db = SessionLocal()\n    survey = db.query(Survey).filter(Survey.id == survey_id).first()\n    responses = db.query(Response).filter(Response.survey_id == survey_id).all()\n    db.close()\n    if not survey or not responses:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=\"Survey or responses not found\")\n\n    columns = [str(q[\"id\"]) for q in survey.questions]\n    data = []\n    for r in responses:\n        row = [r.answers.get(col, \"\") for col in columns]\n        data.append(row)\n    df = pd.DataFrame(data, columns=columns)\n    buf = io.StringIO()\n    df.to_csv(buf, index=False)\n    buf.seek(0)\n    return FileResponse(io.BytesIO(buf.getvalue().encode()), media_type=\"text/csv\", survey_id).first()\n    responses = db.query(Response).filter(Response.survey_id == survey_id).all()\n    db.close()\n    if not survey or not responses:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=\"Survey or responses not found\")\n\n    buf = io.BytesIO()\n    doc = SimpleDocTemplate(buf, pagesize=letter)\n    styles = getSampleStyleSheet()\n    elements = [Paragraph(f\"Survey Report: {survey.title}\", styles['Title']),\n                Paragraph(survey.description, styles['Normal']),\n                Spacer(1, 12)]\n    columns = [str(q[\"id\"]) for q in survey.questions]\n    data = [columns]\n    for r in responses:\n        row = [str(r.answers.get(col, \"\")) for col in columns]\n        data.append(row)\n    table = Table(data)\n    elements.append(table)\n    doc.build(elements)\n    buf.seek(0)\n    return FileResponse(buf, media_type=\"application/pdf\", filename=\"survey_report.pdf\")\n\n# --- Minimal React Frontend (place in ./frontend/src/App.js) ---\n\"\"\"\nimport React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';\n\nconst API = \"http://localhost:8000\";\n\nfunction App() {\n  const [surveys, setSurveys] = useState([]);\n  const [selected, setSelected] = useState(null);\n  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState([{id: 1, text: \"\", type: \"scale\", options: []}]);\n  const [responses, setResponses] = useState([]);\n  const [answers, setAnswers] = useState({});\n  const [chartUrl, setChartUrl] = useState(\"\");\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    fetch(API + \"/surveys/\").then(r => r.json()).then(setSurveys);\n  }, []);\n\n  const Survey\",\n        description: \"A demo survey.\",\n        questions\n      })\n    }).then(r => r.json()).then(s => setSurveys([...surveys, s]));\n  };\n\n  const selectSurvey = (id) => {\n    setSelected(id);\n    fetch(API + `/responses/${id}`).then(r => r.json()).then(setResponses);\n    setChartUrl(API + `/analysis/radar/${id}`);\n  };\n\n  const submitResponse = () => {\n    fetch(API + \"/responses/\", {\n      method: \"POST\",\n      headers: {\"Content-Type\": \"application/json\"},\n      body: JSON.stringify({survey_id: selected, answers})\n    }).then(r => r.json()).then(r => setResponses([...responses, r]));\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{padding:20}}>\n      <h2>Surveys</h2>\n      <button onClick={createSurvey}>Create Demo Survey</button>\n      <ul>\n        {surveys.map(s => <li key={s.id}>\n          <button onClick={() => selectSurvey(s.id)}>{s.title}</button>\n        </li>)}\n      </ul>\n      {selected && <>\n        <h3>Responses</h3>\n        <ul>\n          {responses.map(r => <li key={r.id}>{JSON.stringify(r.answers)}</li>)}\n        </ul>\n        <h3>Submit Response</h3>\n        {surveys.find(s => s.id === selected)?.questions.map(q </div>\n        ))}\n        <button onClick={submitResponse}>Submit</button>\n        <h3>Radar Chart</h3>\n        <img src={chartUrl} alt=\"Radar Chart\" style={{maxWidth:400}} />\n        <h3>Download Reports</h3>\n        <a href={API + `/report/csv/${selected}`}>CSV</a> | <a href={API + `/report/pdf/${selected}`}>PDF</a>\n      </>}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n\nexport default                         "# app.py\n\"\"\"\nA minimal Python MVP for survey capture, analysis, and reporting.\nBackend: Flask (APIs for survey management, data export)\nFrontend: React (served via static files)\nVisualization: Radar chart & heatmap (via Chart.js in React)\nPDF/CSV export: Flask endpoints\n\nTo run:\n1. Install dependencies: pip install flask flask-cors pandas reportlab\n2. Place the React frontend build in ./frontend/build\n3. Run: python app.py\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport io\nimport csv\nfrom flask import Flask, request, jsonify, send_file, send_from_directory\nfrom flask_cors import CORS\nimport pandas as pd\nfrom reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter\nfrom reportlab.pdfgen import canvas\n\napp = Flask(__name__, static_folder='frontend/build', static_url_path='')\nCORS(app)\n\n# --- In-memory storage (for MVP) ---\nSURVEYS = {}  # survey_id: {name, questions: [{id, text, type}], responses: [{answers}]}\nSURVEY_COUNTER = 1\nQUESTION_COUNTER = 1\n\n# --- API Endpoints ---\n\n@app.route('/api/surveys', methods=['GET'])\ndef list_surveys():\n    return jsonify([\n        {\n            'id': sid,\n            'name': s['name'],\n            'num_questions': len(s['questions']),\n            'num_responses': len(s['responses'])\n        }\n        for sid, s in SURVEYS.items()\n    ])\n\n@app.route('/api/surveys', methods=['POST'])\ndef create_survey():\n    global SURVEY_COUNTER, QUESTION_COUNTER\n    data = request.json\n    name = data.get('name')\n    questions = data.get('questions', [])\n    survey_id = str(SURVEY_COUNTER)\n    SURVEY_COUNTER += 1\n    # Assign question IDs\n    qs = []\n    for q in questions:\n        qid = str(QUESTION_COUNTER)\n        QUESTION_COUNTER += 1\n        qs.append({'id': qid, 'text': q['text'], 'type': q.get('type', 'scale')})\n [q[\"id\"] for q in questions]\n    data = []\n    for r in RESPONSES.get(survey_id, []):\n        row = [r[\"answers\"].get(qid, np.nan) for qid in q_ids]\n        data.append(row)\n    df = means})\n\n@app.route('/api/surveys/<survey_id>/heatmap', methods=['GET'])\ndef heatmap_data(survey_id):\n    \"\"\"\n    Returns correlation matrix between questions for heatmap.\n    Output: {labels: [str], matrix: [[float]]}\n    \"\"\"\n    df, questions = get_response_df(survey_id)\n    if df is None or df.empty:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"No data\"}), 400\n    corr =   download_name=f\"survey_{survey_id}_responses.csv\")\n\n@app.route('/api/surveys/<survey_id>/report.pdf', methods=['GET'])\ndef pdf_report(survey_id):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generates a PDF report with pdf.cell(0, 10, \"Radar Chart:\", ln=1)\n\n    # Save radar chart temporarily to insert into PDF\n    img_path = f\"/tmp/{uuid.uuid4()}.png\"\n    with open(img_path, \"wb\") as f:\n        f.write(img_buf.read())\n    pdf.image(img_path, x=10, y=30, w=100)\n    os.remove(img_path)\n    pdf.ln(70)\n    pdf.cell(0, 10, \"Responses Summary:\", ln=1)\n    pdf.set_font(\"Arial\", size=10)\n Delete\n        resp = self.client.delete(f\"/api/surveys/{sid}\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.get_json()[\"status\"], \"deleted\")\n        # Get after delete\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{sid}\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n\n    def test_submit_and_list_responses(self):\n        sid, questions = self.create_survey()\n        # No responses yet\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{sid}/radar\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n        # Add responses\n        self.submit_response(sid, \"u1\", {\"q1\": 2, \"q2\": 4})\n        self.submit_response(sid, \"u2\", {\"q1\": 4, \"q2\": 2})\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{sid}/radar\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"labels\"], [q[\"text\"] for q in questions])\n        # Means: q1: (2+4)/2=3, q2: (4+2)/2=3\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"values\"], [3.0, 3.0])\n\n    def test_heatmap_data(self):\n        sid, questions = self.create_survey()\n        # No responses yet\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{sid}/heatmap\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n        # Add responses\n        self.submit_response(sid, \"u1\", {\"q1\": 1, \"q2\": 2})\n        self.submit_response(sid, \"u2\", {\"q1\": 2, \"q2\": 1})\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{sid}/heatmap\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"labels\"], [q[\"text\"] for q in questions])\n        # The correlation matrix for two questions with values [1,2] and [2,1] is [[1,-1],[-1,1]]\n        matrix = data[\"matrix\"]\n        self.assertEqual(len(matrix), 2)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(matrix[0][0], 1.0)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(matrix[1][1], 1.0)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(matrix[0][1], -1.0)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(matrix[1][0], -1.0)\n\n    def test_csv_report(self):\n        sid, questions = self.create_survey()\n        self.submit_response(sid, \"alice\", {\"q1\": 5, \"q2\": 3})\n        self.submit_response(sid, \"bob\", {\"q1\": 2, \"q2\": 1})\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{sid}/report.csv\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.mimetype, \"text/csv\")\n        # CSV report should be valid (just respondent)\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{sid}/report.csv\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        content = resp.data.decode(\"utf-8\")\n        self.assertIn(\"respondent\", content)\n        # PDF report should be valid\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{sid}/report.pdf\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n\n    def test_edge_case_missing_answers(self):\n        sid, questions = self.create_survey()\n        # --- Data Analysis ---\n\n    def test_radar_data(self):\n        survey_id, questions = self.create_sample_survey()\n        self.submit_response(survey_id, \"A\", {\"q1\": 1, \"q2\": 2})\n        self.submit_response(survey_id, \"B\", {\"q1\": 3, \"q2\": 4})\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/radar\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"labels\"], [q[\"text\"] for q in questions])\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(data[\"values\"][0], 2.0)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(data[\"values\"][1], 3.0)\n\n    def test_heatmap_data(self):\n        survey_id, questions = self.create_sample_survey()\n        self.submit_response(survey_id, \"A\", {\"q1\": 1, \"q2\": 2})\n        self.submit_response(survey_id, \"B\", {\"q1\": 3, \"q2\": 4})\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/heatmap\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"labels\"], [q[\"text\"] for q in questions])\n        # Correlation matrix should be 2x2\n        self.assertEqual(len(data[\"matrix\"]), 2)\n        self.assertEqual(len(data[\"matrix\"][0]), 2)\n        # Diagonal should be 1\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(data[\"matrix\"][0][0], 1.0)\n\n    def test_radar_no_data(self):\n        survey_id, _ = self.create_sample_survey()\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/radar\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n\n    def test_heatmap_no_data(self):\n        survey_id, _ = self.create_sample_survey()\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/heatmap\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n\n    def test_analysis_on_nonexistent_survey(self):\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/api/surveys/invalid_id/radar\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/api/surveys/invalid_id/heatmap\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n\n    #                         "import unittest\nimport json\nfrom io import BytesIO\nfrom app import app, SURVEYS, RESPONSES\n\nclass SurveyMVPTestCase(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.app = app.test_client()\n        # Clear in-memory storage before each test\n        SURVEYS.clear()\n        RESPONSES.clear()\n\n    def create_sample_survey(self, title=\"Test Survey\", questions=None):\n        if questions is None:\n            questions = [\n                {\"id\": \"q1\", \"text\": \"Clarity\", \"type\": \"number\"},\n                {\"id\": \"q2\", \"text\": \"Depth\", \"type\": \"number\"},\n                {\"id\": \"q3\", \"text\": \"Fun\", \"type\": \"number\"}\n            ]\n        resp = self.app.post(\n            \"/api/surveys\",\n            data=json.dumps({\"title\": title, \"questions\": questions}),\n            content_type=\"application/json\"\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 201)\n        survey_id = resp.get_json()[\"survey_id\"]\n        return survey_id, questions\n\n    def submit_response(self, survey_id, respondent, answers):\n        resp = self.app.post(\n            f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/responses\",\n            data=json.dumps({\"respondent\": respondent, \"answers\": answers}),\n            content_type=\"application/json\"\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 201)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.get_json()[\"status\"], \"submitted\")\n\n    # --- Survey Management Tests ---\n\n    def test_create_and_list_survey(self):\n        survey_id, questions = self.create_sample_survey()\n        # List surveys\n        resp = self.app.get(\"/api/surveys\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(data), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(data[0][\"id\"], survey_id)\n        self.assertEqual(data[0][\"title\"], \"Test Survey\")\n        self.assertEqual(data[0][\"questions\"], questions)\n\n    def test_get_survey(self):\n        survey_id, questions = self.create_sample_survey()\n        resp = self.app.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"title\"], \"Test Survey\")\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"questions\"], questions)\n\n    def test_get_survey_not_found(self):\n        resp = self.app.get(\"/api/surveys/doesnotexist\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n\n    def test_delete_survey(self):\n        survey_id, _ = self.create_sample_survey()\n        resp = self.app.delete(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.get_json()[\"status\"], \"deleted\")\n        # Should not be found anymore\n        resp = self.app.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n\n    # --- Survey Response Tests ---\n\n    def test_submit_and_list_responses(self):\n        survey_id, questions = self.create_sample_survey()\n        self.submit_response(survey_id, \"alice\", {\"q1\": 5, \"q2\": 4, \"q3\": 3})\n        self.submit_response(survey_id, \"bob\", {\"q1\": 2, \"q2\": 3, \"q3\": 1})\n        # List responses\n        resp = self.app.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/responses\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(data), 2)\n        self.assertEqual(data[0][\"respondent\"], \"alice\")\n        self.assertEqual(data[1][\"respondent\"], \"bob\")\n        self.assertEqual(data[0][\"answers\"][\"q1\"], 5)\n        self.assertEqual(data[1][\"answers\"][\"q3\"], 1)\n\n    def test_submit_response_to_nonexistent_survey(self):\n        resp = self.app.post(\n            \"/api/surveys/doesnotexist/responses\",\n            data=json.dumps({\"respondent\": \"x\", \"answers\": {\"q1\": 1}}),\n            content_type=\"application/json\"\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n\n    def test_list_responses_nonexistent_survey(self):\n        resp = self.app.get(\"/api/surveys/doesnotexist/responses\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n\n    def test_submit_response_missing_answers(self):\n        survey_id, _ = self.create_sample_survey()\n        # answers missing: should default to empty dict\n        resp = self.app.post(\n            f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/responses\",\n            data=json.dumps({\"respondent\": \"anon\"}),\n            content_type=\"application/json\"\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 201)\n        # Should be present in responses\n        resp = self.app.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/responses\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(data[0][\"respondent\"], \"anon\")\n        self.assertEqual(data[0][\"answers\"], {})\n\n    # --- Data Analysis Tests ---\n\n    def test_radar_data(self):\n        survey_id, questions = self.create_sample_survey()\n        self.submit_response(survey_id, \"a\", {\"q1\": 5, \"q2\": 3, \"q3\": 1})\n        self.submit_response(survey_id, \"b\", {\"q1\": 1, \"q2\": 2, \"q3\": 3})\n        resp = self.app.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/radar\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"labels\"], [q[\"text\"] for q in questions])\n        self.assertEqual(len(data[\"values\"]), 3)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(data[\"values\"][0], 3.0)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(data[\"values\"][1], 2.5)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(data[\"values\"][2], 2.0)\n\n    def test_radar_data_no_responses(self):\n        survey_id, _ = self.create_sample_survey()\n        resp = self.app.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/radar\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n\n    def test_radar_data_nonexistent_survey(self):\n        resp = self.app.get(\"/api/surveys/doesnotexist/radar\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n\n    def test_heatmap_data(self):\n        survey_id, questions = self.create_sample_survey()\n        self.submit_response(survey_id, \"a\", {\"q1\": 5, \"q2\": 3, \"q3\": 1})\n        self.submit_response(survey_id, \"b\", {\"q1\": 1, \"q2\": 2, \"q3\": 3})\n        resp = self.app.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/heatmap\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"labels\"], [q[\"text\"] for q in questions])\n        self.assertEqual(len(data[\"matrix\"]), 3)\n        self.assertEqual(len(data[\"matrix\"][0]), 3)\n        # Header row should include respondent and all q ids\n        for q in [\"respondent\"] + [q[\"id\"] for q in questions]:\n            self.assertIn(q, content)\n        self.assertIn(\"alice\", content)\n        self.assertIn(\"bob\", content)\n        self.assertIn(\"1,2,3\", content.replace(\"\\r\", \"\"))  #                         "import unittest\nimport json\nfrom io import BytesIO\nfrom app import app, SURVEYS, RESPONSES\n\nclass SurveyMVPTestCase(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.client = app.test_client()\n        # Clear in-memory data before each test\n        SURVEYS.clear()\n        RESPONSES.clear()\n\n    def create_sample_survey(self, title=\"Test Survey\"):\n        questions = [\n            {\"id\": \"q1\", \"text\": \"Quality\", \"type\": \"number\"},\n            {\"id\": \"q2\", \"text\": \"Speed\", \"type\": \"number\"},\n            {\"id\": \"q3\", \"text\": \"Satisfaction\", \"type\": \"number\"}\n        ]\n        resp = self.client.post(\n            \"/api/surveys\",\n            data=json.dumps({\"title\": title, \"questions\": questions}),\n            content_type=\"application/json\"\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 201)\n        survey_id = resp.get_json()[\"survey_id\"]\n        return survey_id, questions\n\n    def submit_response(self, survey_id, respondent, answers):\n        resp = self.client.post(\n            f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/responses\",\n            data=json.dumps({\"respondent\": respondent, \"answers\": answers}),\n            content_type=\"application/json\"\n        )\n        return resp\n\n    # --- Survey Management ---\n\n    def test_create_and_list_survey(self):\n        survey_id, questions = self.create_sample_survey()\n        # List surveys\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/api/surveys\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        surveys = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(surveys), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(surveys[0][\"id\"], survey_id)\n        self.assertEqual(surveys[0][\"title\"], \"Test Survey\")\n        self.assertEqual(surveys[0][\"questions\"], questions)\n\n    def test_get_and_delete_survey(self):\n        survey_id, questions = self.create_sample_survey()\n        # Get survey\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        survey = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(survey[\"title\"], \"Test Survey\")\n        self.assertEqual(survey[\"questions\"], questions)\n        # Delete survey\n        resp = self.client.delete(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.get_json()[\"status\"], \"deleted\")\n        # Get deleted survey\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n\n    def test_get_nonexistent_survey(self):\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/api/surveys/doesnotexist\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n\n    # --- Survey Response ---\n\n    def test_submit_and_list_responses(self):\n        survey_id, questions = self.create_sample_survey()\n        # Submit response\n        resp = self.submit_response(survey_id, \"alice\", {\"q1\": 5, \"q2\": 3, \"q3\": 4})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 201)\n        # List responses\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/responses\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        responses = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(responses), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(responses[0][\"respondent\"], \"alice\")\n        self.assertEqual(responses[0][\"answers\"], {\"q1\": 5, \"q2\": 3, \"q3\": 4})\n\n    def test_submit_response_to_nonexistent_survey(self):\n        resp = self.submit_response(\"doesnotexist\", \"bob\", {\"q1\": 1})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n\n    def test_list_responses_for_nonexistent_survey(self):\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/api/surveys/doesnotexist/responses\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n\n    def test_submit_response_missing_answers(self):\n        survey_id, questions = self.create_sample_survey()\n        # Submit with missing answers (should default to NaN)\n        resp = self.submit_response(survey_id, \"bob\", {})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 201)\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/responses\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        responses = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(responses[0][\"answers\"], {})\n\n    # --- Data Analysis ---\n\n    def test_radar_and_heatmap_data(self):\n        survey_id, questions = self.create_sample_survey()\n        # No responses yet\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/radar\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n        resp = self.client.get(f\"/api/surveys/{survey_id}/heatmap\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n        # survey_id: {title, questions}\nRESPONSES = {}    # survey_id: [ {respondent, answers: {q_id: value}} ]\n\n\n# --- Survey Management APIs ---\n\n@app.route('/api/surveys', methods=['POST'])\ndef create_survey():\n    \"\"\"Create a new survey with title and questions.\"\"\"\n    data = request.json\n    survey_id = str(uuid.uuid4())\n    # Each question must have a unique id (frontend should ensure this)\n    SURVEYS[survey_id] = {\n        \"title\": data.get(\"title\", \"\"),\n        \"questions\": data.get(\"questions\", [])  # [{id, text, type}]\n    }\n    RESPONSES[survey_id] = []\n    return jsonify({\"survey_id\": survey_id}), 201\n\n@app.route('/api/surveys', methods=['GET'])\ndef list_surveys():\n    \"\"\"List all surveys.\"\"\"\n    return jsonify([\n        {\"id\": sid, \"title\": s[\"title\"], \"questions\": s[\"questions\"]}\n        for sid, s in SURVEYS.items()\n    ])\n\n@app.route('/api/surveys/<survey_id>', methods=['GET'])\ndef get_survey(survey_id):\n    \"\"\"Get a specific survey.\"\"\"\n    survey = SURVEYS.get(survey_id)\n    if not survey:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Survey not found\"}), 404\n    return jsonify(survey)\n\n@app.route('/api/surveys/<survey_id>', methods=['DELETE'])\ndef delete_survey(survey_id):\n    \"\"\"Delete a survey and its responses.\"\"\"\n    SURVEYS.pop(survey_id, None)\n    RESPONSES.pop(survey_id, None)\n    return jsonify({\"status\": \"deleted\"})\n\n\n# --- Survey Response API ---\n\n@app.route('/api/surveys/<survey_id>/responses', methods=['POST'])\ndef submit_response(survey_id):\n    \"\"\"Submit a response to a survey.\"\"\"\n    data = request.json\n    if survey_id not in SURVEYS:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Survey not found\"}), 404\n    RESPONSES[survey_id].append({\n        \"respondent\": data.get(\"respondent\", \"anonymous\"),\n        \"answers\": data.get(\"answers\", {})  # {q_id: value}\n    })\n    return jsonify({\"status\": \"submitted\"}), 201\n\n@app.route('/api/surveys/<survey_id>/responses', methods=['GET'])\ndef list_responses(survey_id):\n    \"\"\"List all responses for a survey.\"\"\"\n    if survey_id not in SURVEYS:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Survey not found\"}), 404\n    return jsonify(RESPONSES.get(survey_id, []))\n\n\n# --- Data Analysis APIs ---\n\ndef get_response_df(survey_id):\n    \"\"\"Convert responses to DataFrame (questions as columns).\"\"\"\n    survey = SURVEYS.get(survey_id)\n    if not survey:\n        return None, None\n    questions = survey[\"questions\"]\n    q_ids = [q[\"id\"] for q in questions]\n    data = []\n    for r in RESPONSES.get(survey_id, []):\n        row = [r[\"answers\"].get(qid, np.nan) for qid in q_ids]\n        data.append(row)\n    df = pd.DataFrame(data, columns=q_ids)\n    return df, questions\n\n@app.route('/api/surveys/<survey_id>/radar', methods=['GET'])\ndef radar_data(survey_id):\n    \"\"\"\n    Return data for radar chart:\n    {\n      \"labels\": [question text...],\n      \"values\": [mean for each question...]\n    }\n    \"\"\"\n    df, questions = get_response_df(survey_id)\n    if df is None or df.empty:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"No data\"}), 400\n    means = df.mean(numeric_only=True).fillna(0).tolist()\n    labels = [q[\"text\"] for q in questions]\n    return jsonify({\"labels\": labels, \"values\": means})\n\n@app.route('/api/surveys/<survey_id>/heatmap', methods=['GET'])\ndef heatmap_data(survey_id):\n    \"\"\"\n    Return data for heatmap:\n    {\n      \"labels\": [question text...],\n      \"matrix\": [[correlation matrix]]\n    }\n    \"\"\"\n    df, questions = get_response_df(survey_id)\n    if df is None or df.empty:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"No data\"}), 400\n    # Only numeric columns for correlation\n    corr = df.corr().fillna(0)\n    labels = [q[\"text\"] for q in questions]\n    return jsonify({\"labels\": labels, \"matrix\": corr.values.tolist()})\n\n\n# --- Report Generation ---\n\n@app.route('/api/surveys/<survey_id>/report.csv', methods=['GET'])\ndef csv_report(survey_id):\n    \"\"\"Return survey responses as CSV.\"\"\"\n    df, questions = get_response_df(survey_id)\n    if df is None:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Survey not found\"}), 404\n    respondents = [r[\"respondent\"] for r in RESPONSES[survey_id]]\n    df.insert(0, \"respondent\", respondents)\n    buf = BytesIO()\n    df.to_csv(buf, index=False)\n    buf.seek(0)\n    return send_file(\n        buf,\n        mimetype='text/csv',\n        as_attachment=True,\n        download_name=f\"survey_{survey_id}_responses.csv\"\n    )\n\n@app.route('/api/surveys/<survey_id>/report.pdf', methods=['GET'])\ndef pdf_report(survey_id):\n    \"\"\"Generate a PDF report with radar chart and responses.\"\"\"\n    df, questions = get_response_df(survey_id)\n    if df is None:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Survey not found\"}), 404\n    survey = SURVEYS[survey_id]\n    # Radar chart\n    means = df.mean(numeric_only=True).fillna(0).tolist()\n    labels = [q[\"text\"] for q in questions]\n    N = len(labels)\n    if N == 0:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"No questions in survey\"}), 400\n    angles = np.linspace(0, 2 * np.pi, N, endpoint=False).tolist()\n    means_plot = means + means[:1]\n    angles_plot = angles + angles[:1]\n\n    fig = plt.figure(figsize=(4, 4))\n    ax = fig.add_subplot(111, polar=True)\n    ax.plot(angles_plot, means_plot, 'o-', linewidth=2)\n    ax.fill(angles_plot, means_plot, alpha=0.25)\n    ax.set_thetagrids(np.degrees(angles), labels)\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    img_buf = BytesIO()\n    plt.savefig(img_buf, format='png', bbox_inches='tight')\n    plt.close(fig)\n    img_buf.seek(0)\n\n    # PDF generation\n    pdf = FPDF()\n    pdf.add_page()\n    pdf.set_font(\"Arial\", size=16)\n    pdf.cell(0, 10, f\"Survey Report: {survey['title']}\", ln=1)\n    pdf.set_font(\"Arial\", size=12)\n    pdf.cell(0, 10, \"Radar Chart:\", ln=1)\n    # Save radar chart to temp file for FPDF\n    img_path = f\"/tmp/{uuid.uuid4()}.png\"\n    with open(img_path, \"wb\") as f:\n        f.write(img_buf.read())\n    pdf.image(img_path, x=10, y=30, w=100)\n    os.remove(img_path)\n    pdf.ln(70)\n    pdf.cell(0, 10, \"Responses Summary:\", ln=1)\n    pdf.set_font(\"Arial\", size=10)\n    # Table of responses\n    respondents = [r[\"respondent\"] for r in RESPONSES[survey_id]]\n    for idx, row in df.iterrows():\n        ans = \", \".join([f\"{questions[i]['text']}: {row[q['id']]}\" for i, q in enumerate(questions)])\n        pdf.multi_cell(0, 8, f\"Respondent: {respondents[idx]}, Answers: {ans}\")\n    # Output PDF\n    pdf_buf = BytesIO(pdf.output(dest='S').encode('latin1'))\n    pdf_buf.seek(0)\n    return send_file(\n        pdf_buf,\n        mimetype='application/pdf',\n        as_attachment=True,\n        download_name=f\"survey_{survey_id}_report.pdf\"\n    )\n\n\n# --- Main ---\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app.run(debug=True)\n\n\n\"\"\"\n--- React Frontend (Create React App) ---\n\n1. Setup:\n    npx create-react-app survey-mvp\n    cd survey-mvp\n    npm install axios recharts react-heatmap-grid\n\n2.                         "import unittest\nimport json\nimport io\nimport tempfile\nfrom app import app, SURVEYS, RESPONSES\n\nclass SurveyAPITestCase(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.client = app.test_client()\n        # Clear in-memory storage before each test\n        SURVEYS.clear()\n        RESPONSES.clear()\n\n    def create_survey(self, title=\"Test Survey\", questions=None):\n        if questions is None:\n            questions = [\n                {\"text\": \"Q1\", \"type\": \"number\"},\n                {\"text\": \"Q2\", \"type\": \"number\"}\n            ]\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/surveys', json={\"title\": title, \"questions\": questions})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 201)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertIn(\"survey_id\", data)\n        return data[\"survey_id\"]\n\n    def submit_response(self, survey_id, respondent=\"user\", answers=None):\n        if answers is None:\n            # Use correct question ids\n            questions = SURVEYS[survey_id][\"questions\"]\n            answers = {q[\"id\"]: 5 for q in questions}\n        resp = self.client.post(f'/api/surveys/{survey_id}/responses', json={\n            \"respondent\": respondent,\n            \"answers\": answers\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 201)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.get_json()[\"status\"], \"submitted\")\n\n    # --- Survey Management ---\n\n    def test_create_and_list_surveys(self):\n        survey_id = self.create_survey()\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/surveys')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(s[\"id\"] == survey_id for s in data))\n\n    def test_create_survey_missing_fields(self):\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/surveys', json={})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"error\", resp.get_json())\n\n    def test_get_survey(self):\n        survey_id = self.create_survey()\n        resp = self.client.get(f'/api/surveys/{survey_id}')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"title\"], \"Test Survey\")\n\n    def test_get_nonexistent_survey(self):\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/surveys/doesnotexist')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n\n    def test_delete_survey(self):\n        survey_id = self.create_survey()\n        resp = self.client.delete(f'/api/surveys/{survey_id}')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.get_json()[\"status\"], \"deleted\")\n        # Ensure deleted\n        resp = self.client.get(f'/api/surveys/{survey_id}')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n\n    def test_delete_nonexistent_survey(self):\n        resp = self.client.delete('/api/surveys/doesnotexist')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n\n    # Add responses with correlation\n        qids = [q[\"id\"] for q in SURVEYS[survey_id][\"questions\"]]\n        self.submit_response(survey_id, answers={qids[0]: 1, qids[1]: 2})\n        self.submit_response(survey_id, answers={qids[0]: 2, qids[1]: 4})\n        self.submit_response(survey_id, answers={qids[0]: 3, qids[1]: 6})\n        resp = self.client.get(f'/api/surveys/{survey_id}/heatmap')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(data[\"labels\"]), 2)\n        self.assertEqual(len(data[\"matrix\"]), 2)\n        # self.submit_sample_response(survey_id, \"user1\", {qids[0]: \"abc\", qids[1]: 5})\n        resp = self.client.get(f'/api/surveys/{survey_id}/radar')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n 5)\n\n    def test_response_with_missing_question_answers(self):\n        survey_id = self.create_sample_survey()\n        qids = [q[\"id\"] for q in SURVEYS[survey_id][\"questions\"]]\n        # Only answer one question\n        self.submit_sample_response(survey_id, \"user1\", {qids[0]: 7})\n        resp = self.client.get(f'/api/surveys/{survey_id}/radar')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        # Second value should be 0 (NaN filled as 0)\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"values\"][0], 7)\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"values\"][1], 0)\n\n    def test_multiple_surveys_independent(self):\n        # Create two surveys\n        sid1 = self.create_sample_survey()\n        sid2 = self.create_sample_survey()\n        self.assertNotEqual(sid1, sid2)\n        # Responses for each are independent\n        qids1 = [q[\"id\"] for q in SURVEYS[sid1][\"questions\"]]\n        qids2 = [q[\"id\"] for q in SURVEYS[sid2][\"questions\"]]\n        self.submit_sample_response(sid1, \"user1\", {qids1[0]: 1, qids1[1]: 2})\n        self.submit_sample_response(sid2, \"user2\", {qids2[0]: 3, qids2[1]: 4})\n        resp1 = self.client.get(f'/api/surveys/{sid1}/responses')\n        resp2 = self.client.get(f'/api/surveys/{sid2}/responses')\n        self.assertEqual(len(resp1.get_json()), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(len(resp2.get_json()), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(resp1.get_json()[0][\"respondent\"], \"user1\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp2.get_json()[0][\"respondent\"], \"user2\")\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    unittest.main()",
